     <ea-hero background-color="none" image-large="https://media.contentapi.ea.com/content/dam/eacom/SIMS/images/2018/05/ts4-hero-medium-packs-ep5-7x2-xl.jpg.adapt.crop5x2.1455w.jpg" image-largest="https://media.contentapi.ea.com/content/dam/eacom/SIMS/images/2018/05/ts4-hero-medium-packs-ep5-7x2-xl.jpg.adapt.crop7x2.1920w.jpg" image-medium="https://media.contentapi.ea.com/content/dam/eacom/SIMS/images/2018/05/ts4-hero-medium-packs-ep5-7x2-xl.jpg.adapt.crop2x1.1023w.jpg" image-small="https://media.contentapi.ea.com/content/dam/eacom/SIMS/images/2018/05/ts4-hero-medium-packs-ep5-7x2-xl.jpg.adapt.crop3x5.767w.jpg" image-smallest="https://media.contentapi.ea.com/content/dam/eacom/SIMS/images/2018/05/ts4-hero-medium-packs-ep5-7x2-xl.jpg.adapt.crop3x5.320w.jpg" image-tooltip="" layout="medium" logo-image="https://media.contentapi.ea.com/content/dam/eacom/SIMS/PC/common/ts4-ep5-home-hero-medium-logo-v3.png" scrim-color="none" scrim-opacity="medium" spacing-bottom="medium" subtitle-text="Jahreszeiten ist jetzt erhältlich!" text-align="center" text-color="dark" text-position="left">
      <h2>

       <h1>

       </h1>
       <h2>
        Die Sims 4
        <span>
         PC
        </span>
